 ITR daakhil karne ke liye 31 agast tak kaa hi samay heitiar daakhil nahin kiya to lag saktaa he 5 hajaar tak kaa jurmanagalat itiar form bharne se bachanaa chahieinakam tex ritern (ITR) daakhil karne ke liye 31 agast tak kaa hi samay he yani aaj ko lekar teen din hi bache hai
 For those who have not yet filed income tax returns, there is still a chance, do it immediately
 itiar daakhil karnaa ab online hone se kaaphi aasaan ho gaya he, iske baavjood agar aapako dikkat mahasoos ho rahi ho to kisi chartered accountint kii madad leni chahie
 If you come under the tax net and you have not filed ITR, then the Income Tax Department can impose a fine of up to Rs 5000
 iskar ritern kaa form aapako bahut saavdhaanee se bharna hoga
 For your convenience, we are talking about five common mistakes that people often make
 aisi galatiyon se bachakar aap sahi tareeke se ritern kaa form bhar sakate hai
 1
 galat itiar form bharnatex or nivesh export balavant jain bataate hai, 'sabase pehle aapako yah jaananaa chahie ki aapako koun-sa itiar form bharna he
 If the wrong form is filled then the entire exercise will be of no use
 zyaadaatar logon ko itiar-1 bharna hota he, jise sahaj kaha jaataa he
 If you are an individual taxpayer whose total annual income is less than Rs 50 lakh (from all sources), then you have to fill this form
 lekin agar 50 lakh rupee se zyada kii salanaa aay he, ek se zyada houseng property he, kisi company main diarectorship he, capital gains se inakam he, videsh se koi inakam he to aapako ITR-2 bharna hoga
 'individuals or Hindu Undivided Families (HUF) earning income from a business or profession have to file ITR-3
 2
 Not to mention income from other sources, other than salary or business income, you must also tell the income from other sources
 seaving bank kaa intrest saamaanya logon ke liye 10,000 rupee or senior citigen ke liye 50,000 tak texable aay se mukt he, lekin isaki jaankaree aapako inakam main dikhaakar didction clem karnaa hota he
 If TDS is deducted on FD, then you should also inform about it
 agar aap jaankaree chhipaayenge to penalty bhi lag sakati he
 This can range from 50 to 200 percent of tax evasion
 naaballig bacchon kii aay kii bhi jaankaree jarur deni chahie
 Minor is an active income like income from a TV show will be taxable for the child, but is a passive income, such as if there is income from an investment in his name, then it is tax free up to Rs 1500 annually, more than the mother or Will be added to the father's income (whoever has more income)
 log mutual fund yaa sheyaron se hone vaale capital gains bataanaa kai baar bhul jate hai, capital gains kaa vivaran bharte samay sailareed log zyada galati karte hai, kyonki unke liye isaki jaankaree kaaphi jatil lagati he
 So if you have income from capital gains then the help of a professional CA must be taken
 3
 Do not give information about more than one house, if there is more than one house, then you cannot use ITR-1 form
 aapako ITR-2 bharna hoga
 If there is a self occupation of more than one house, then according to the rule of the last year, only one house will be exempted, for the other house, the rental income will be given at the market rate on which 30% deduction is also given
 4
 Do not update contact details, it is very important that you update your email ID and phone number
 aajkal iskar vibhaag sampark i-mail yaa phone ke dwaara hi karata he
 Keep in mind that do not give the email ID or phone number received by the employer, but give your personal email or phone number, because your personal contact will work only if you leave the job
 5
 Not to give details of all bank accounts, details of all bank accounts should be given in the income tax return
 itiar ke form main detail bharen to usamen bank acount bahut saavdhaanee se bharen kyonki aajkal rifund sidhe acount main hi online aata he
 Therefore, in the ITR, you have to give details about which account you want the refund
